Hootsuite Is Building A Learning Community"},"title":{"type":"text","value":"Why Hootsuite Is Building A Learning Community"},"body":{"type":"text","value":"<h1 class=\"jn b jo jv ch\"><span style=\"color:rgba(0, 0, 0, 1);\">Why Hootsuite Is Building A Learning Community</span></h1>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"9942\"><strong class=\"lu mg\">Hootsuite has experienced tremendous growth over the past five years. When you&rsquo;re in growth mode and scaling globally, it&rsquo;s critical that you have a team of adaptable learners who are up for all the challenges and opportunities growth presents. An essential ingredient for creating an adaptable organization is building a learning community, where we continually challenge ourselves and grow our capabilities.</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"031b\">Every day we are closing the distance between where we are and where we want to be, individually and as an organization. We become better employees, leaders, customers, and people through work challenges and opportunities we face daily.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"89ec\">Many organizations talk about the importance of learning and intuitively, we understand how it can help us deliver results. But practically, aside from conceptually believing in the importance of learning, we want to create a community that makes learning part of how we work. We want to excel at learning and sharing knowledge and, more importantly, changing how we behave because of what we learned.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"0af1\">At the risk of sounding like a Hallmark card, this is a development journey and we are constantly practicing, failing, and getting feedback for growth. Learning isn&rsquo;t something separate from who we are or how we work every day. We use the demands of the business to stretch ourselves, learning every day, in every way we do our jobs. The demands of the business challenge us to overcome our own limitations and grow.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"c8ff\">It&rsquo;s a community, full of people supporting your practice, rooting for your success, contributing to your learning, and learning from you. But that same community is going to push you, and so are the processes and the ways the organization works.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"47f4\">The idea of a learning community may be new to some. These are the principles that define and guide our efforts, and will help you get a feel for what it&rsquo;s like to work in this environment.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"6f93\"><strong class=\"lu mg\">Principles of the Learning Community</strong></p>\n\n<ol>\n\t<li class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf mh mi mj\" id=\"1fc0\">There is no finish line &mdash; growth is a continual practice.</li>\n\t<li class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv mk lx ml lz mm mb mn md mo mf mh mi mj\" id=\"68ac\">Our weaknesses and limitations can be an asset because they represent the greatest potential for growth.</li>\n\t<li class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv mk lx ml lz mm mb mn md mo mf mh mi mj\" id=\"1c8f\">Learning and development is not a separate process &mdash; it must be integrated into how we work every day. Stand-alone learning experiences like courses have a purpose but do not form the foundation of the learning community.</li>\n\t<li class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv mk lx ml lz mm mb mn md mo mf mh mi mj\" id=\"eccd\">The growth of the organization and the growth of individuals are interdependent. Growth of the individual is the fuel for organizational growth.</li>\n\t<li class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv mk lx ml lz mm mb mn md mo mf mh mi mj\" id=\"ce5c\">Progress requires support and challenge. It won&rsquo;t always feel comfortable.</li>\n\t<li class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv mk lx ml lz mm mb mn md mo mf mh mi mj\" id=\"47a5\">Development and learning are everybody&rsquo;s responsibility. Everybody has dual roles &mdash; teacher and learner. Hierarchy does not change participation.</li>\n\t<li class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv mk lx ml lz mm mb mn md mo mf mh mi mj\" id=\"50e1\">There are no passengers on this journey and there are definitely no spectators. Nobody gets a hall pass, regardless of their role. Working in a learning community means preparing for continual practice, understanding what you are good at and what challenges and prevents you from learning, and delivering your very best. You will need humility to see your limitations, those areas that need to grow. Most importantly, your passion for learning must be matched by your desire to share your learning, to challenge and support others to grow.</li>\n</ol>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"9eba\">We&rsquo;re in the early days of building this new approach to learning and development at Hootsuite. We&rsquo;ll be sharing our learnings as we go, as well as stories for our team on how the learning community impacts their work. Much more to come. If you are interested in learning more about the ideas behind our learning community, check out a book called <a class=\"dc bt mp mq mr ms\" href=\"https://www.amazon.ca/Everyone-Culture-Deliberately-Developmental-Organization/dp/1625278624\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\"><strong class=\"lu mg\">An Everyone Culture: Becoming a Deliberately Developmental Organization.</strong></a></p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"8d93\">You can find all of Hootsuite&rsquo;s <a class=\"dc bt mp mq mr looks like at Hootsuite for developers. I was interested in getting to work with more cutting edge technologies and experiencing a positive workplace culture.</p>\n\n<p class=\"lp lq ch ap lr b ls lt lu lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc\" id=\"2f55\">The technologies I get to work with here enable us to develop software code using programming languages designed with simplicity in mind. I&rsquo;ve also had the opportunity to write code to build and change infrastructure with versioning&mdash;which has been a cool experience.</p>\n\n<blockquote class=\"mi\">\n<div class=\"mj mk ml ap jn b ke mm mn mo mp mq mc\" id=\"59ac\">\n<p class=\"jn b mr ms at\">&ldquo;Connecting the work we do with making an impact is innate to my team.&rdquo;</p>\n</div>\n</blockquote>\n\n<figure class=\"mt mu mv mw mx ev x y paragraph-image\">\n<div class=\"my mz ej na ab\">\n<div class=\"x y ac\">\n<div class=\"lj l ej lk\">\n<div class=\"nb l\">\n<div class=\"do lg gi n o gh ab bx lh li\"><img alt=\"undefined\" src=\"https://cdn.phenompeople.com/CareerConnectResources/HOOTUS/images/Thomas-blog-team-1579605000748.jpeg\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto;\" /></div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n\n<figcaption class=\"at eb nc nd hj dm x y ne nf ao cy\">Some team members and me after a bootcamp session at HQ</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\n<p class=\"lp lq ch ap lr b ls lt lu lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc\" id=\"4458\"><strong class=\"lr md\">What excites you about coming to work every day?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"lp lq ch ap lr b ls lt lu lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc\" id=\"9e16\">I always look forward to the opportunity to work on challenging problems that impact customers &mdash; while working with smart, passionate, egoless colleagues. One of the things I love most about the culture now that I&rsquo;m at Hootsuite has to be the egoless environment. I think this plays a big part in allowing us to work effectively and efficiently together.</p>\n\n<p class=\"lp lq ch ap lr b ls lt lu lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc\" id=\"2fda\">For example, there was a day where we had an issue with one of the systems my team is responsible for, and one of my colleagues&mdash;without prompt&mdash;asked how they could help. This colleague was already incredibly busy with existing work but decided to put the team&rsquo;s needs first.</p>\n\n<figure class=\"lr ls lt lu lv fw he nx cv ny nz oa ob oc bs cx od oe of og aw paragraph-image\">\n<div class=\"no np bi nq ab\">\n<div class=\"x y nw\">\n<div class=\"lz l bi ma\">\n<div class=\"nr l\"><img alt=\"undefined\" src=\"https://cdn.phenompeople.com/CareerConnectResources/HOOTUS/images/Thomas-blog-mountain-1579605032562.jpeg\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto;\" /></div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n\n<figcaption class=\"as bg ns nt ii ek x y nu nv an ec\" data-selectable-paragraph=\"\">Another proud accomplishment: after 12 hours of hiking Black Tusk!</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\n<p class=\"lp lq ch ap lr b ls lt lu lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc\" id=\"48f8\"><strong class=\"lr md\">What has been your best accomplishment at Hootsuite so far?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"lp lq ch ap lr b ls lt lu lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc\" id=\"0094\">One accomplishment that stands out is working with my team to redesign and implement a system, which ultimately allowed for easier mechanisms in providing features to customers based on what they have paid for.</p>\n\n<p class=\"lp lq ch ap lr b ls lt lu lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc\" id=\"b725\">I like knowing that the work I do impacts customers because it then allows me to develop the right things. In the same way that understanding your audience when writing an article is important; there is no difference when it comes to developing software. Knowing who you are building something for is key.</p>\n\n<p class=\"lp lq ch ap lr b ls lt lu lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc\" id=\"10d5\">Connecting the work we do with making an impact is innate to my team; we are responsible for the systems that maintain customer&rsquo;s billing and entitlements.</p>\n\n<p class=\"lp lq ch ap lr b ls lt lu lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc\" id=\"d749\"><strong class=\"lr md\">What are some examples of the problems you get to solve at work?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"lp lq ch ap lr b ls lt lu lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc\" id=\"2cd7\">We solve new problems every single day at Hootsuite. My work usually will involve finding answers to the following questions:</p>\n\n<ol>\n\t<li class=\"lp lq ch ap lr b ls lt lu lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc nt nu nv\" id=\"41fe\">How do we integrate our existing service with external services in a flexible and scalable manner?</li>\n\t<li class=\"lp lq ch ap lr b ls nw lu nx lw ny ly nz ma oa mc nt nu nv\" id=\"0db3\">How do we migrate data from one system to another with minimal to no impact?</li>\n</ol>\n\n<p class=\"lp lq ch ap lr b ls lt lu lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc\" id=\"9955\"><strong class=\"lr md\">What does learning and growth look like for a software developer at Hootsuite?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"lp lq ch ap lr b ls lt lu lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc\" id=\"02d9\">Hootsuite provides many avenues for learning and growth for a developer, from having a dedicated learning budget to offering a dynamic mentorship program.</p>\n\n<p class=\"lp lq ch ap lr b ls lt lu lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc\" id=\"63db\">I&rsquo;ve taken advantage of what Hootsuite offers on several occasions. This includes everything from being able to attend an industry conference to purchasing new technical books to grow my skills.</p>\n\n<p class=\"lp lq ch ap lr b ls lt lu lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc\" id=\"debe\">I believe that learning doesn&rsquo;t need to stop after finishing one&rsquo;s formal education; it&rsquo;s a lifelong journey. One of the biggest things I have learned in my time at Hootsuite is how to provide constructive and inclusive feedback when reviewing someone&rsquo;s software code. The ability to provide feedback in a respectful and helpful manner is something I&rsquo;ll be able to apply to all aspects of my life and future.</p>\n\n<hr class=\"ob cy gz oc od hj oe of og oh oi\" problems at Hootsuite Bucharest with Mihai, staff developer"},"title":{"type":"text","value":"Solving problems at Hootsuite Bucharest with Mihai, staff developer"},"body":{"type":"text","value":"<h1 class=\"ka b kb ki ch\">Solving problems at Hootsuite Bucharest with Mihai, staff developer</h1>\n\n<h2 class=\"ao cy kr ks at\">Mihai joined Hootsuite Bucharest through an acquisition in 2014. Since then, he&rsquo;s worked on everything from building new products to leading teams in more than one country. Keep reading to uncover Mihai&rsquo;s greatest career moments and collect his insights on learning at Hootsuite.</h2>\n\n<figure class=\"lo lp lq lr ls ev x y paragraph-image\">\n<div class=\"jl jm ej jn ab\">\n<div class=\"x y ln\">\n<div class=\"jr l ej js\">\n<div class=\"lt l\">\n<div class=\"do jo gi n o gh ab bx jp jq\"><img alt=\"undefined\" src=\"https://cdn.phenompeople.com/CareerConnectResources/HOOTUS/images/Mihai1-1579604612506.png\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto;\" /></div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n\n<figcaption class=\"at eb lu lv hj dm x y lw lx ao cy\">A few peeps enjoying the terrace at at the Bucharest office</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\n<p class=\"ly lz ch ap ma b mb mc md me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml\" id=\"a50b\"><strong class=\"ma mm\">A little about me</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"ly lz ch ap ma b mb mc md me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml\" id=\"db26\">I&rsquo;m someone who enjoys challenges, sports, and everything tech. Learning and doing new things every day is the reason I wake up in the morning.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ly lz ch ap ma b mb mc md me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml\" id=\"ca00\">I started my career at Hootsuite Bucharest as a junior developer through the acquisition of (what&rsquo;s formerly) UberVU in 2014. So far, I&rsquo;ve built two products from scratch, rebranded one, worked with a new team in a different country, and had a lot of fun doing it all. My role now is staff developer.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ly lz ch ap ma b mb mc md me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml\" id=\"7924\"><strong class=\"ma mm\">You recently had the opportunity to work in Hootsuite&rsquo;s Toronto office for five months! Tell us more about that experience.</strong></p>\n\n<figure class=\"lo lp lq lr ls ev gf mo br mp mq mr ms mt bc mu mv mw mx my mz paragraph-image\">\n<div class=\"jl jm ej jn ab\">\n<div class=\"x y mn\">\n<div class=\"jr l ej js\">\n<div class=\"na l\">\n<div class=\"do jo gi n o gh ab bx jp jq\">&nbsp;</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</figure>\n\n<p class=\"ly lz ch ap ma b mb mc md me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml\" id=\"cbec\"><img alt=\"undefined\" src=\"https://cdn.phenompeople.com/CareerConnectResources/HOOTUS/images/Mihai2-1579604645928.jpeg\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto;\" />About a year ago, Hootsuite acquired a New York company called LiftMetrix. The plan was to hire a team of developers in Toronto to help expand the product.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ly lz ch ap ma b mb mc md me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml\" id=\"b0fa\">The idea was to bring over the infrastructure and processes that we built in Bucharest for Hootsuite Analytics, and onboard the new development team in Toronto. Our teams had different technologies, techniques and processes &mdash; so the goal was to unify the team and share our knowledge.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ly lz ch ap ma b mb mc md me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml\" id=\"0407\"><strong class=\"ma mm\">What were some of the challenges that came with that opportunity?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"ly lz ch ap ma b mb mc md me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml\" id=\"57a5\">Everything was new! Which meant everything was an adventure. I was on my own &mdash; new city, new people, and a new routine. I was definitely out of my comfort zone. By the end of the five months, I ended up getting to know lots of people, making friends, and loving the city. It was bittersweet returning to Romania.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ly lz ch ap ma b mb mc md me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml\" id=\"9b58\">I also needed to work at a global level &mdash; my manager was based in New York while I was still working with my team in Bucharest. I learned a lot about working across time zones, being efficient with my time and remaining conscious of other offices.</p>\n\n<blockquote class=\"nb\">\n<div class=\"nc nd ne ap ka b kr nf ng nh ni nj ml\" id=\"ebf8\">\n<p class=\"ka b nk nl at\">That&rsquo;s the mindset I&rsquo;ve learned to have. Give things time, relax, and have fun solving whatever problem you are facing. Enjoy the process, you&rsquo;ll get there.</p>\n</div>\n</blockquote>\n\n<p class=\"ly lz ch ap ma b mb nm md nn mf no mh np mj nq ml\" id=\"f6cd\"><strong class=\"ma mm\">What has been one of your greatest career moments so far?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"ly lz ch ap ma b mb mc md me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml\" id=\"42ab\">Building Hootsuite Analytics. It was a great challenge because I was 21 at the time, and we built everything from scratch. I worked on both API and data acquisition. I had the opportunity to work with so many teams internally &mdash; people from Vancouver, the go-to-market team for the launch, and probably others I&rsquo;m missing. Everything was new &mdash; the team, the challenges. The whole experience was really a defining moment in my career.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ly lz ch ap ma b mb mc md me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml\" id=\"179f\">Launching Hootsuite Analytics was a huge accomplishment. We were monitoring the users and had a buzzer go off every time the number went up &mdash; there was a real joy and excitement in the office that day. We sat together monitoring systems, errors, and everything went perfectly.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ly lz ch ap ma b mb mc md me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml\" id=\"82ca\"><strong class=\"ma mm\">What is one unique thing about working at Hootsuite?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"ly lz ch ap ma b mb mc md me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml\" id=\"de22\">We work in an environment where it&rsquo;s safe to experiment and make mistakes.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ly lz ch ap ma b mb mc md me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml\" id=\"13f8\"><strong class=\"ma mm\">Do you have an example of a time you made a mistake?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"ly lz ch ap ma b mb mc md me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml\" id=\"1e50\">Oh yes. When we were building Hootsuite Analytics, we could deploy using a chat bot. One time I was attempting to deploy from my phone and in doing so, I killed all the servers for about 10&ndash;15 minutes. After that, we improved our system so that a mistake like that was no longer possible.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ly lz ch ap ma b mb mc md me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml\" id=\"306d\">I should add that we try to foster an environment where people aren&rsquo;t scared of mistakes. Our approach for dealing with broken systems is a knowledge source that shouldn&rsquo;t be discouraged.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ly lz ch ap ma b mb mc md me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml\" id=\"ad0e\"><strong class=\"ma mm\">How have you prepared for each new position you&rsquo;ve moved into at Hootsuite?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"ly lz ch ap ma b mb mc md me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml\" id=\"8382\">I try to learn as much as I can in my everyday work and get involved in bigger projects. I also make an effort to spend one hour every day learning about a particular topic that is relevant to a problem we are trying to solve.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ly lz ch ap ma b mb mc md me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml\" id=\"2a88\">My co-workers play a key role as well: we do code reviews, pair programming, share articles and tech talks, and have lunch discussions. It still amazes me how much I learn only by going for lunch with my team.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ly lz ch ap ma b mb mc md me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml\" id=\"5fb5\"><strong class=\"ma mm\">Where do you go to stay up to date?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"ly lz ch ap ma b mb mc md me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml\" id=\"dbb7\">I watch a lot of YouTube &mdash; channels like the GOTO Conferences, CNCF (Cloud Native Computing Foundation), Kubernetes, and Strange Loop. I also read blogs like High Scalability, and the developer blogs from companies like Google, Uber, and Facebook.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ly lz ch ap ma b mb mc md me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml\" id=\"1406\"><strong class=\"ma mm\">What has been the most notable thing you&rsquo;ve learned from a mentor?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"ly lz ch ap ma b mb mc md me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml\" id=\"a831\">Everything has a solution, we just need to have the right mindset to look for the best one. We should embrace problems, not avoid them. That&rsquo;s the fun part of my work now. What we work on is complicated, but we can improve everything.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ly lz ch ap ma b mb mc md me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml\" id=\"0473\">That&rsquo;s the mindset I&rsquo;ve learned to have. Give things time, relax, and have fun solving whatever problem you are facing. Enjoy the process, you&rsquo;ll get there.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ly lz ch ap ma b mb mc md me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml\" id=\"9f6b\"><strong class=\"ma mm\">What advice would you give to people who are early in their careers or new to Hootsuite?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"ly lz ch ap ma b mb mc md me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml\" id=\"5938\">Just have fun. There are a lot of interesting projects and challenges to keep you from getting bored and learning. Look for what you find interesting, and do more of that.</p>\n\n<hr class=\"nr cy gz ns nt hj nu nv nw nx ny\" />\n<p class=\"ly lz ch ap ma b mb mc md me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml\" id=\"7615\"><strong class=\"ma mm\">Interested in solving problems at Hootsuite? </strong><a class=\"dc bt nz oa ob oc\" href=\"http://ow.ly/b8mA30jyaRJ\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\"><strong class=\"ma mm\">We&rsquo;re id=\"0265\">Our <a class=\"dc bt lr ls lt lu\" href=\"http://ow.ly/oCUE30koeQF\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\">sales team</a> at Hootsuite is ever-evolving. Naturally, we wanted to connect with Lisa White, director of our commercial sales team in London. Read on to hear how her and her team are making an impact at Hootsuite.</p>\n\n<figure class=\"lw lx ly lz ma ev x y paragraph-image\">\n<div class=\"jl jm ej jn ab\">\n<div class=\"x y lv\">\n<div class=\"jr l ej js\">\n<div class=\"mb l\">\n<div class=\"do jo gi n o gh ab bx jp jq\">&nbsp;</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</figure>\n\n<p class=\"ld le ch ap lf b lg lh li lj lk ll lm ln lo lp lq\" id=\"cd03\"><strong class=\"lf mc\"><img alt=\"undefined\" src=\"https://cdn.phenompeople.com/CareerConnectResources/HOOTUS/images/LisaFamily-1579604436034.jpeg\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto;\" />Tell us a bit about your career path leading up to Hootsuite.</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"ld le ch ap lf b lg lh li lj lk ll lm ln lo lp lq\" id=\"3f17\">When I graduated from university, I wanted to pursue a career in PR and marketing. Thankfully, the organisation I was working for insisted all team members have a stint on the sales floor to learn about the products they were plugging. I loved selling so much I never headed back to the marketing department!</p>\n\n<p class=\"ld le ch ap lf b lg lh li lj lk ll lm ln lo lp lq\" id=\"9a38\">It also taught me how valuable it is to understand the product you&rsquo; working with. From there, I moved into front line small- and medium-sized business (SMB) and enterprise (ENT) sales where I really developed a passion for sales. As with any sales person who consistently exceeds their sales quota, I was recognised for my success and made the move into sales management. I&rsquo;ve been responsible for guiding SMB and ENT teams selling to every continent in the world which led me to my current role here at <a class=\"dc bt lr ls lt lu\" href=\"/hootsuite-careers/inside-hootsuite-london-4889d58db9da\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\">Hootsuite London</a>.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ld le ch ap lf b lg lh li lj lk ll lm ln lo lp lq\"><img alt=\"undefined\" src=\"https://cdn.phenompeople.com/CareerConnectResources/HOOTUS/images/Lisa2-1579604489686.jpeg\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto;\" /></p>\n\n<figure class=\"lw lx ly lz ma ev x y paragraph-image\">\n<div class=\"jl jm ej jn ab\">\n<div class=\"x y md\">\n<div class=\"jr l ej js\">\n<div class=\"me l\">\n<div class=\"do jo gi n o gh ab bx jp jq\">&nbsp;</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</figure>\n\n<p class=\"ld le ch ap lf b lg lh li lj lk ll lm ln lo lp lq\" id=\"5c3f\"><strong class=\"lf mc\">What excites you about social media and how do you know you&rsquo;re making an impact?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"ld le ch ap lf b lg lh li lj lk ll lm ln lo lp lq\" id=\"54cc\">Social media is such a huge aspect of everyday life and connects us all &mdash; it&rsquo;s so exciting how social media is constantly evolving! One of the best parts is how diverse the companies and verticals we work with are, and no two prospects are the same. This means we&rsquo;re constantly learning, and our day-to-day is always different and interesting.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ld le ch ap lf b lg lh li lj lk ll lm ln lo lp lq\" id=\"c192\"><strong class=\"lf mc\">How would you describe your management style? Do you have any particular leadership philosophy?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"ld le ch ap lf b lg lh li lj lk ll lm ln lo lp lq\" id=\"126b\">I&rsquo;ve managed teams in multiple countries, and have had exposure to different people with different backgrounds, cultures, influences and ambitions &mdash; I think it&rsquo;s imperative to adopt a chameleon style of management. No two people are the same and that goes for team members too! Everyone works differently and I tailor my management style to suit the needs of my individual team members, nurturing each one to achieve their maximum potential in a way that works for them.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ld le ch ap lf b lg lh li lj lk ll lm ln lo lp lq\" id=\"9beb\"><strong class=\"lf mc\">What are some ways you grow the capabilities of your team and support career development?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"ld le ch ap lf b lg lh li lj lk ll lm ln lo lp lq\" id=\"0b2b\">My role is to coach my team to be as successful as possible in their position. This enables them to reach the next step in their career. Every team member has different goals and ambitions, so I tailor their coaching to support that. For example, if someone wants to move into management, I get them to mentor new starters. Whereas someone wanting to move into sales training, I ask them to lead a team training initiative.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ld le ch ap lf b lg lh li lj lk ll lm ln lo lp lq\" id=\"3c38\"><strong class=\"lf mc\">What could a career path look like for a commercial account executive?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"ld le ch ap lf b lg lh li lj lk ll lm ln lo lp lq\" id=\"1989\">Being a successful salesperson in software as a service (SAAS) and especially in social media opens doors to move in any direction. CAE&rsquo;s typically move into a field sales role but can also move into sales training, customer success, team leadership, or product marketing. Take your pick!</p>\n\n<p class=\"ld le ch ap lf b lg lh li lj lk ll lm ln lo lp lq\" id=\"9d13\"><strong class=\"lf mc\">What goals do you and your team have right now? How do you plan on achieving those results?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"ld le ch ap lf b lg lh li lj lk ll lm ln lo lp lq\" id=\"562b\">Growth is always our number one goal! The team really pulled together in Q1 to deliver some fantastic results, and now our goal for the next quarter is to double it.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ld le ch ap lf b lg lh li lj lk ll lm ln lo lp lq\" id=\"6383\"><strong class=\"lf mc\">What are some of the competencies that make a successful CAE?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"ld le ch ap lf b lg lh li lj lk ll lm ln lo lp lq\" id=\"e2e8\">Each member of the team owns their tasks and responsibilities, whilst simultaneously maintaining the capacity to mentor and help out others. Everyone is responsible for hitting their own targets, but we also pull together as a team and support each other to get there.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ld le ch ap lf b lg lh li lj lk ll lm ln lo lp lq\" id=\"dafa\"><strong class=\"lf mc\">What types of companies do you work with? What kind of markets are your team exposed to?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"ld le ch ap lf b lg lh li lj lk ll lm ln lo lp lq\" id=\"5a6e\">One of the most fantastic things about Hootsuite &mdash; and what&rsquo;s really amazing about our product &mdash; is that any business with a social media strategy can benefit from our service. This means we get exposure to fascinating companies of all types and sizes, working in all kinds of markets. The sky&rsquo;s the limit in terms of opportunities, so we&rsquo;re always kept very busy!</p>\n\n<p class=\"ld le ch ap lf b lg lh li lj lk ll lm ln lo lp lq\" id=\"0dfd\"><strong class=\"lf mc\">How would you describe the work environment at Hootsuite London?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"ld le ch ap lf b lg lh li lj lk ll lm ln lo lp lq\" id=\"5211\">Hootsuite London is one of those places you just can&rsquo;t wait to get into each morning. I always get in a little early and start my day walking past some of London&rsquo;s most famous and historic landmarks right on Hootsuite&rsquo;s doorstep. The city of London comes into view once you enter the building and find yourself faced with one of the most impressive views of the London skyline the city has to offer.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ld le ch ap lf b lg lh li lj lk ll lm ln lo lp lq\" id=\"70e5\">This serenity doesn&rsquo;t last long &mdash; Hootsuite is full of enthusiastic, motivated and interesting people. There&rsquo;s always a buzz and sense of energy around the workplace. The nest is a performance-driven and collaborative environment. Everyone is extremely approachable and happy to help each other out.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ld le ch ap lf b lg lh li lj lk ll lm ln lo lp lq\" id=\"18bb\"><strong class=\"lf mc\">What excites you most about the upcoming year, and the future of Hootsuite and social media?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"ld le ch ap lf b lg lh li lj lk ll lm ln lo lp lq\" id=\"ffd8\">I&rsquo;m so excited for the growth and expansion we have in place for 2018. Watching the success of each team member is the greatest reward, and the entire team is headed for great things this year!</p>\n\n<hr class=\"mf cy gz mg mh hj mi mj mk ml mm\" />\n<p class=\"ld le ch ap lf b lg lh li lj lk ll lm ln lo lp lq\" id=\"f1b6\"><strong class=\"lf mc\">Interested in working with Lisa? Hootsuite"},"body":{"type":"text","value":"<h1 class=\"jn b jo jv ch\">Building a career through building relationships with Paige, product manager at Hootsuite</h1>\n\n<h2 class=\"ao cy ke kf at\">From customer support advocate to product liaison, to now product manager, Paige sheds some light on her career journey at Hootsuite.</h2>\n\n<figure class=\"lb lc ld le lf ev x y paragraph-image\">\n<div class=\"lg lh ej li ab\">\n<div class=\"x y la\">\n<div class=\"lm l ej ln\">\n<div class=\"lo l\">\n<div class=\"do lj gi n o gh ab bx lk ll\">&nbsp;</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</figure>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"428f\"><strong class=\"lu mg\"><img alt=\"undefined\" src=\"https://cdn.phenompeople.com/CareerConnectResources/HOOTUS/images/Paige1-1579595755136.jpeg\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto;\" />A little about me</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"0275\">I&rsquo;m warm, easy to get to know, and I love connecting with people &mdash; especially over something delicious. I enjoy facing challenges head-on and solving problems, as each one is another opportunity to learn something new. I&rsquo;m inspired by new experiences, meeting creative minds, and seeing the work they do &mdash; it&rsquo;s why I love coming to work every day. In my time at Hootsuite, I&rsquo;ve had the amazing opportunity to collaborate and build relationships with many mentors, colleagues, and friends.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"155b\"><strong class=\"lu mg\">Describe your career path so far.</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"bdb7\">I joined Hootsuite in 2013 as a customer support advocate. After graduating from university, I worked in retail customer service before a good friend introduced me to Hootsuite. I&rsquo;m very fortunate that Hootsuite took a chance on hiring me to its customer support team during its hyper-growth phase.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"299e\">Back then, we were a small team so I had to quickly learn all of the intricate ins-and-outs of the product through talking to our customers. Through this, I developed an interest in the product and a passion for advocating for our customers. In 2015, I became the product liaison and built relationships with the product management and development teams in prioritizing bugs and feature requests on behalf of our customers.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"1f7a\">Product management wasn&rsquo;t on my radar and I never imagined it&rsquo;d be an option for me. A mentor &mdash; and more importantly friend &mdash; took the career jump from product liaison to the product department which opened a new door for me. Inspired to follow in her footsteps, I took my experience from participating in the 2016 pilot of the <a class=\"dc bt mh mi mj mk\" href=\"https://www.linkedin.com/pulse/unexpected-way-stop-people-from-quitting-ryan-holmes/\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\">stretch program</a>. This provided an environment where I could experience the role firsthand and helped me confidently solidify my next career step.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"c014\">I&rsquo;ve been on the product team for just over a year. I continue to learn so much every day through collaborating with colleagues and discovering more about our customers &mdash; all of which has helped shape me into the product manager I am today.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\"><img alt=\"undefined\" src=\"https://cdn.phenompeople.com/CareerConnectResources/HOOTUS/images/Paige2-1579595820515.jpeg\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto;\" /></p>\n\n<figure class=\"lr ls lt lu lv fw x y paragraph-image\">\n<div class=\"lw lx bi ly ab\">\n<div class=\"x y nb\">\n<div class=\"mc l bi md\">\n<div class=\"nc l\">&nbsp;</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</figure>\n\n<blockquote class=\"mn\">\n<div class=\"mo mp mq ap jn b ke mr ms mt mu mv mf\" id=\"0307\">\n<p class=\"jn b mw mx at\">&ldquo;I know for a fact I wouldn&rsquo;t have learned everything that&rsquo;s made me into the product manager I am today without the humans of Hootsuite.&rdquo;</p>\n</div>\n</blockquote>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv my lx mz lz na mb nb md nc mf\" id=\"bf07\"><strong class=\"lu mg\">Having had multiple roles within the company, how have you prepared for each new step?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"8985\">I start by stretching the scope of my current job by finding ways to take on extra projects and responsibilities.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"4676\">When I was a customer advocate, I took on a specialization in our mobile platform, making me the point person for all mobile-related questions for the support team. I also began helping the current product liaison, and this set me up to take over her role when she made the transition to the product team.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"7c56\">When I took over the product liaison role, I found an opportunity to improve the bug triage and resolution process, and implemented a new system across teams. This helped me grow my communication skills and began training me to make data-driven decisions in preparation for my next role at Hootsuite.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"3589\">Though it definitely takes some extra work and commitment, working on these side projects are what uncovered new skills to work on and introduced me to something new I could see myself doing.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"5257\"><strong class=\"lu mg\">How has working at Hootsuite helped accelerate your career?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"cffc\">Hootsuite took a chance on me, and provided opportunities to learn over the years. I&rsquo;ve been set up for success through support from management, coaching, and training. My experience has been working in an environment where I&rsquo;m encouraged to ask questions, and learn from my mistakes so I can continue growing my professional career.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"266d\"><strong class=\"lu mg\">What has been your greatest learning (or most memorable moment) at Hootsuite so far?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"aff2\">It&rsquo;s probably no surprise at this point, but it&rsquo;s the people. I learn best through firsthand experience and connecting with people &mdash; Hootsuite has given me the opportunity to do both. I know for a fact I wouldn&rsquo;t have learned everything that&rsquo;s made me into the product manager I am today without the humans of Hootsuite.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\"><img alt=\"undefined\" src=\"https://cdn.phenompeople.com/CareerConnectResources/HOOTUS/images/Paige3-1579595859930.jpeg\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto;\" /></p>\n\n<figure class=\"lb lc ld le lf ev x y paragraph-image\">\n<div class=\"lg lh ej li ab\">\n<div class=\"x y nd\">\n<div class=\"lm l ej ln\">\n<div class=\"ne l\">\n<div class=\"do lj gi n o gh ab bx lk ll\"><strong class=\"lu mg\">How have your co-workers been a part of your learning experiences?</strong></div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</figure>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"453a\">I treasure the relationships I&rsquo;ve built with each and every single colleague. Being a part of teams where I know I&rsquo;m trusted and supported has allowed me to take chances and grow.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"5e51\">Most importantly, many of my coworkers (both past and present) have become some of my closest friends, and I know I wouldn&rsquo;t be where I am today without them.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"b4ae\">By getting to know my coworkers and understanding what they do, I&rsquo;m always assured that if I don&rsquo;t know the answer to something, I always know who to go to.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"912d\"><strong class=\"lu mg\">What advice would you give to people who are interested in beginning a career journey at Hootsuite?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"1199\">Be open. Talk to new people and hear their stories. Take on new experiences that might be challenging but rewarding. Navigate a career path that works for you no matter how windy it might be.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"4397\">The most inspiring question I&rsquo;ve come to love asking fellow owls is, &ldquo;How did you get to where you are now?&rdquo; Everyone&rsquo;s answer is so different, and further reinforces there isn&rsquo;t one way to achieve success.</p>\n\n<hr class=\"nf cy gz ng nh hj ni nj nk nl nm\" />\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"5261\"><strong class=\"lu mg\">Interested in beginning your career at Hootsuite? </strong><a class=\"dc bt mh mi mj mk\" href=\"http://ow.ly/xhFD30j6r2r\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\"><strong class=\"lu mg\">We&rsquo;re trusting yourself is your greatest career advantage \u2014 with Camille, solutions consultant"},"title":{"type":"text","value":"Why trusting yourself is your greatest career advantage \u2014 with Camille, solutions consultant"},"body":{"type":"text","value":"<h1 class=\"jn b jo jv ch\"><span style=\"color:rgba(0, 0, 0, 1);\"><strong class=\"bb\">Why trusting yourself is your greatest career advantage &mdash; with Camille, solutions consultant</strong></span></h1>\n\n<blockquote class=\"ls\">\n<div class=\"lt lu lv ap jn b lw lx ly lz ma mb mc\" id=\"e7e9\">\n<p class=\"jn b md me at\">&ldquo;I&rsquo;ve learned to just ride an invisible surfboard through life&rsquo;s waves of challenges. Stand as strong as your feet can hold, look that wave right in the eye, and fight like hell on the way down.&rdquo;</p>\n</div>\n</blockquote>\n\n<p class=\"mf mg ch ap mh b mi mj mk ml mm mn mo mp mq mr mc\" id=\"2d3b\"><strong class=\"mh ms\">Tell us about you.</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"mf mg ch ap mh b mi mt mk mu mm mv mo mw mq mx mc\" id=\"31ea\">Feel the fear and do it anyway. Ever since I heard that phrase, I&rsquo;ve repeated it every time I&rsquo;ve faced a challenge. This best describes who I am and the approach I take to most things.</p>\n\n<p class=\"mf mg ch ap mh b mi mt mk mu mm mv mo mw mq mx mc\" id=\"750a\">I&rsquo;ve learned to trust three things in life: <strong class=\"mh ms\">my instinct, my work ethic and the process. </strong>I trust my instinct because it tells me what to do, I trust my work ethic because it gets me where I want to go and I always,<em class=\"my\"> always</em> trust the process because every situation has an unknown factor that we must surrender to. This comes back to feeling the fear and doing it anyway. One must live past fear, in order to trust anything at all. OK, that was really deep&hellip; Haha! While I love a good philosophical debate, I also love to dance, sing, write, and chill with cool, creative people.</p>\n\n<figure class=\"kz la lb lc ld ev gf na br nb nc nd ne nf bc ng nh ni nj nk nl paragraph-image\">\n<div class=\"lg lh ej li ab\">\n<div class=\"x y mz\">\n<div class=\"lm l ej ln\">\n<div class=\"nm l\">\n<div class=\"do lj gi n o gh ab bx lk ll\">&nbsp;</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n\n<figcaption class=\"at eb nn no hj dm x y np nq ao cy\"><img alt=\"undefined\" src=\"https://cdn.phenompeople.com/CareerConnectResources/HOOTUS/images/Camille-blog-family-1579609112778.jpeg\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto;\" />My awesome fam!</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\n<p class=\"mf mg ch ap mh b mi mt mk mu mm mv mo mw mq mx mc\" id=\"f300\">Above all, my husband and two kids are everything to me. My life got exponentially better the day I met Roger. He&rsquo;s my rock and my partner in everything &mdash; life, love, and business. Chase and Marley who just turned seven and three (they were born on the same day &mdash; nope, not planned!) are two of the most wildly intelligent, loving little humans I have the great honour of leading through life. Having them actually brought me closer to my own mom and my siblings. We&rsquo;ve created a village around them, both in person and virtually. And because of that, they approach everyone they meet with their heart wide open.</p>\n\n<p class=\"mf mg ch ap mh b mi mt mk mu mm mv mo mw mq mx mc\" id=\"890a\"><strong class=\"mh ms\">What did you do prior to joining Hootsuite?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"mf mg ch ap mh b mi mt mk mu mm mv mo mw mq mx mc\" id=\"8af1\">I&rsquo;ve been a storyteller ever since I learned how to string a sentence together. I&rsquo;m the middle child and have always found ways to capture everyone&rsquo;s attention with a good tale. I used that skill through writing fiction as a teenager and then through TV news stories as a journalist. I worked as a writer and producer in national Canadian television news for nearly 10 years. I love presenting and breaking down complex ideas, and I love presenting them. That&rsquo;s why I started a consulting business where I demystified media for entrepreneurs and small business people, with workshops on how to pitch your story to the press.</p>\n\n<p class=\"mf mg ch ap mh b mi mt mk mu mm mv mo mw mq mx mc\" id=\"df85\">When Roger and I got married, we merged our businesses into a publicity firm called 404 Media Group. We also created a new venture together, an online magazine called <a class=\"dc bt nr ns nt nu\" href=\"https://byblacks.com/\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\">ByBlacks.com</a>. Last year we celebrated five years of this business and received a congratulatory note from Prime Minister Justin Trudeau for the impact we&rsquo;ve had on the Black Canadian community. So, I do a lot outside of my nine to five.</p>\n\n<p class=\"mf mg ch ap mh b mi mt mk mu mm mv mo mw mq mx mc\" id=\"6dfd\">When the Hootsuite opportunity came up, I was really happy they saw all of my other career pursuits and community advocacy as an asset rather than a liability. My role as a solutions consultant at Hootsuite combines my best skills &mdash; communication and advocacy &mdash; in one place and pushes me to grow even more! I made the jump in March 2017 and have zero regrets.</p>\n\n<blockquote class=\"ls\">\n<div class=\"lt lu lv ap jn b lw lx ly lz ma mb mc\" id=\"cab0\">\n<p class=\"jn b md me at\">&ldquo;At Hootsuite, I&rsquo;ve really been able to bring my &ldquo;whole self&rdquo; to the job. That means I don&rsquo;t feel pressured to fit into one way of carrying out my role.&rdquo;</p>\n</div>\n</blockquote>\n\n<p class=\"jn b md me at\">&ldquo;At Hootsuite, I&rsquo;ve really been able to bring my &ldquo;whole self&rdquo; to the job. That means I don&rsquo;t feel pressured to fit into one way of carrying out my role.&rdquo;</p>\n\n<p class=\"mf mg ch ap mh b mi mj mk ml mm mn mo mp mq mr mc\" id=\"4914\"><strong class=\"mh ms\">What has been the greatest learning moment in your career?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"mf mg ch ap mh b mi mt mk mu mm mv mo mw mq mx mc\" id=\"6071\">My first job after graduating from journalism school was at a major TV station. Of course with my youthful ego, I wanted to be the best at everything right away. Frustrated, I asked a more senior journalist if she had any advice for me. She said, &ldquo;Do the small things well.&rdquo; I&rsquo;ve applied that advice to every position I&rsquo;ve taken since then. Even if you&rsquo;re capable of more, always start with the basics and demonstrate that you can do the little things with excellence. That&rsquo;s what invites people to trust you with the bigger things.</p>\n\n<p class=\"mf mg ch ap mh b mi mt mk mu mm mv mo mw mq mx mc\" id=\"130f\"><strong class=\"mh ms\">How have you taken ownership of your career or prepared for new tasks or positions?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"mf mg ch ap mh b mi mt mk mu mm mv mo mw mq mx mc\" id=\"48e4\">Our senior director likes to say, &ldquo;You&rsquo;re the CEO of your desk&rdquo;! And while it may sound too good to be true, it&rsquo;s the real deal at Hootsuite. I&rsquo;ve never worked anywhere that encourages an entrepreneurial spirit at work. At Hootsuite, I&rsquo;ve really been able to bring my &ldquo;whole self&rdquo; to the job. That means I don&rsquo;t feel pressured to fit into one way of carrying out my role.</p>\n\n<p class=\"mf mg ch ap mh b mi mt mk mu mm mv mo mw mq mx mc\" id=\"dd64\">And it&rsquo;s intimidating at first because when you start a new job, your instinct is to fall in line. But once I realized that was not the norm here, I started approaching my customer interactions the way I wanted to be treated if I was on the other end of that call. I started to see my zero experience in software sales explicitly as an advantage instead of a disadvantage. Most of our customers have no clue what we&rsquo;re talking about, unless we really take the time to understand what they care about and meet them where they are at.</p>\n\n<figure class=\"kz la lb lc ld ev x y paragraph-image\">\n<div class=\"lg lh ej li ab\">\n<div class=\"x y nv\">\n<div class=\"lm l ej ln\">\n<div class=\"nw l\">\n<div class=\"do lj gi n o gh ab bx lk ll\"><img alt=\"undefined\" src=\"https://cdn.phenompeople.com/CareerConnectResources/HOOTUS/images/Camille-blog-laptop-1579609185834.jpeg\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto;\" /></div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n\n<figcaption class=\"at eb nn no hj dm x y np nq ao cy\">One of the coolest rooms I&rsquo;ve ever presented in at City University of New York.</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\n<p class=\"mf mg ch ap mh b mi mt mk mu mm mv mo mw mq mx mc\" id=\"908c\"><strong class=\"mh ms\">What adversity have you faced in your career and how have you overcome them?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"mf mg ch ap mh b mi mt mk mu mm mv mo mw mq mx mc\" id=\"7369\">I am an A-type personality and so my greatest challenge is always myself. Battling imposter syndrome and feelings of belonging and worthiness. One moment you feel completely empowered and in control, and the next you feel like you couldn&rsquo;t possibly hold your own. I&rsquo;ve learned to just ride an invisible surfboard through life&rsquo;s waves of challenges. Stand as strong as your feet can hold, look that wave right in the eye, and fight like hell on the way down &mdash; knowing that one way or another, you&rsquo;re gonna come through on the other side.</p>\n\n<p class=\"mf mg ch ap mh b mi mt mk mu mm mv mo mw mq mx mc\"><img alt=\"undefined\" src=\"https://cdn.phenompeople.com/CareerConnectResources/HOOTUS/images/Camille-blog-team-1579609230699.jpeg\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto;\" /></p>\n\n<figure class=\"ny ev nz oa lf le ob paragraph-image\">\n<div class=\"lg lh ej li ab\">\n<div class=\"lm l ej ln\">\n<div class=\"oc l\">\n<div class=\"do lj gi n o gh ab bx lk ll\"><img alt=\"undefined\" src=\"https://cdn.phenompeople.com/CareerConnectResources/HOOTUS/images/Camille-blog-cruise-1579609284335.jpeg\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto;\" /></div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</figure>\n\n<figure class=\"ny ev od oa lf le ob paragraph-image\">\n<div class=\"lg lh ej li ab\">\n<div class=\"lm l ej ln\">\n<div class=\"oe l\">\n<div class=\"do lj gi n o gh ab bx lk ll\">&nbsp;</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n\n<figcaption class=\"at eb nn no hj dm x y np nq ao cy of ej og oh\">These are some of my teammates and I at Toronto&rsquo;s first #hootcruise!</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\n<p class=\"mf mg ch ap mh b mi mt mk mu mm mv mo mw mq mx mc\" id=\"bf27\"><strong class=\"mh ms\">Describe a way you have evolved (in your career or personally) as a result of working at Hootsuite.</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"mf mg ch ap mh b mi mt mk mu mm mv mo mw mq mx mc\" id=\"aab2\">I never considered myself a &lsquo;techy&rsquo; person, I still barely know how to troubleshoot my own computer (ha!). But I&rsquo;ve surprised myself with the depths of new information I&rsquo;ve been able to absorb, understand, and translate impactfully to customers.</p>\n\n<p class=\"mf mg ch ap mh b mi mt mk mu mm mv mo mw mq mx mc\" id=\"9160\">If someone told me that I would go from pitching stories about crime and politics to pitching complex software solutions to customers like Columbia University, the U.S. Marines, the FBI, or the Government of Canada, I would have laughed in their face. But here I am! I&rsquo;ve been with Hootsuite a little over a year now and last quarter I exceeded my sales target by 132 percent. Not bad, considering I didn&rsquo;t know what API stood for before I started working here!</p>\n\n<p class=\"mf mg ch ap mh b mi mt mk mu mm mv mo mw mq mx mc\" id=\"e0d9\">Having a trusting relationship with account executives and customer support managers, and the supportive and collaborative culture of my team (along with incredibly sharp managers) is what allowed me to flourish so quickly at Hootsuite.</p>\n\n<p class=\"mf mg ch ap mh b mi mt mk mu mm mv mo mw mq mx mc\" id=\"6156\"><strong class=\"mh ms\">What advice would you give to people who are early in their careers or new to Hootsuite?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"mf mg ch ap mh b mi mt mk mu mm mv mo mw mq mx mc\" id=\"7761\">You will meet some amazing people, you will meet some challenging people. But <em class=\"my\">you</em> need to show up as the same awesomely smart and kind person no matter who you&rsquo;re dealing with. Don&rsquo;t change yourself to make others feel comfortable. Be flexible and always willing to admit your faults, but take no BS. Ever.</p>\n\n<hr class=\"oi cy gz oj ok hj ol om on oo op\" />\n<p class=\"mf mg ch ap mh b mi mt mk mu mm mv mo mw mq mx mc\" id=\"f04c\"><strong class=\"mh ms\">Interested in taking on a new challenge in your career? </strong><a class=\"dc bt nr ns nt nu\" href=\"http://ow.ly/bsD330lZ71i\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\"><strong class=\"mh ms\">Apply g-headshot"},"size":{"type":"text","value":"large"},"actualsize":{"type":"text","value":188064},"width":{"type":"text","value":1600},"focalPointY":{"type":"text","value":0},"lqip":{"type":"text","value":null},"height":{"type":"text","value":1117},"focalPointX":{"type":"text","value":0}}},"alt":{"type":"text","value":"RD-blog-headshot"}}},"ogTitle":{"type":"text","value":null},"description":{"type":"text","value":"Visionary and tech industry veteran: Meet Hootsuite\u2019s Senior Vice President of Product and Technology"},"title":{"type":"text","value":"Visionary and tech industry veteran: Meet Hootsuite\u2019s Senior Vice President of Product and Technology"},"body":{"type":"text","value":"<h1 class=\"jn b jo jv ch\"><span style=\"color:rgba(0, 0, 0, 1);\">Visionary and tech industry veteran: Meet Hootsuite&rsquo;s Senior Vice President of Product and Technology</span></h1>\n\n<h2 class=\"ao cy ke kf at\">Ryan shares his vision for Hootsuite&rsquo;s product, a 5-year prediction for the industry &mdash; and 3 key traits he looks for when hiring a new team member.</h2>\n\n<p class=\"mc md ch ap me b mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo mp\" id=\"cc26\"><strong class=\"me mq\">Tell us about yourself and your role at Hootsuite.</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"mc md ch ap me b mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo mp\" id=\"b95c\">I&rsquo;m the Senior Vice President of Product and Technology, and have one of the best jobs in the world! I am responsible for leading our incredible product management, user experience, software development, production operations, and security teams as well as ultimately defining the underlying product and technology strategies that constitute Hootsuite&rsquo;s dynamic product portfolio.</p>\n\n<p class=\"mc md ch ap me b mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo mp\" id=\"9192\">This job is a perfect blend of everything I love to do: building world-class marketing technology products, and technically innovating with the latest and greatest cloud technologies, patterns, and practices.</p>\n\n<p class=\"mc md ch ap me b mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo mp\" id=\"0340\"><strong class=\"me mq\">What brought you to Hootsuite?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"mc md ch ap me b mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo mp\" id=\"68d7\">This is actually an interesting story. I had an amazing leadership job at Sitecore, which is one of the world&rsquo;s leaders in digital experience platforms. I had been there for almost five and a half years and seen the company go from single-to-multi-product, from on-premise to cloud, and go through the process of a sale for $1.1B USD to EQT in a record-setting transaction in 2016. And Sitecore is continuing to prosper and do very well in the market. Hence, I wasn&rsquo;t proactively seeking a new opportunity.</p>\n\n<p class=\"mc md ch ap me b mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo mp\" id=\"31d0\">In the back of my mind, I had established an extremely high bar for what my next job would look like. I honestly didn&rsquo;t think I would find it. First, it had to be in the marketing technology space but in a hotter segment than DXPs, which pretty much leaves social.</p>\n\n<p class=\"mc md ch ap me b mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo mp\" id=\"e761\">Second, it had to be with a market-leading company in high-growth mode that is committed to innovation and continued growth and Hootsuite fits this bill perfectly.</p>\n\n<p class=\"mc md ch ap me b mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo mp\" id=\"0e90\">Third, I fell in love with the people and the culture throughout the interview process. And it has been even better actually being here for my first month!</p>\n\n<p class=\"mc md ch ap me b mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo mp\" id=\"54ac\">Lastly, as a Canadian, I am also extremely proud to be once again working for a Canadian company and helping grow the technology sector inside of Canada. Vancouver is one absolute favourite cities in Canada as my mother&rsquo;s family is from Richmond, British Columbia and I have taken three out of the last four vacations in BC.</p>\n\n<figure class=\"ms ev mt mu lp lo mv paragraph-image\">\n<div class=\"lq lr ej ls ab\">\n<div class=\"lw l ej lx\">\n<div class=\"mw l\">\n<div class=\"do lt gi n o gh ab bx lu lv\"><img alt=\"undefined\" src=\"https://cdn.phenompeople.com/CareerConnectResources/HOOTUS/images/RD-blog-vancouver-1579605471606.jpeg\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto;\" /></div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</figure>\n\n<figure class=\"ms ev mt mu lp lo mv paragraph-image\">\n<div class=\"lq lr ej ls ab\">\n<div class=\"lw l ej lx\">\n<div class=\"mw l\">\n<div class=\"do lt gi n o gh ab bx lu lv\"><img alt=\"undefined\" src=\"https://cdn.phenompeople.com/CareerConnectResources/HOOTUS/images/RD-blog-lake-1579605504706.jpeg\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto;\" /></div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n\n<figcaption class=\"at eb mx my hj dm x y mz na ao cy nb ej nc nd\">Some of BC&rsquo;s beautiful landscapes taken by Ryan</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\n<blockquote class=\"ne\">\n<div class=\"nf ng nh ap jn b ke ni nj nk nl nm mp\" id=\"96f7\">\n<p class=\"jn b nn no at\">&ldquo;&hellip;passion, curiosity, and respect. Based on my experience, the healthiest, happiest, and highest performing teams are comprised of individuals that are strong and well-balanced in all three key traits.&rdquo;</p>\n</div>\n</blockquote>\n\n<p class=\"mc md ch ap me b mf np mh nq mj nr ml ns mn nt mp\" id=\"fc08\"><strong class=\"me mq\">What&rsquo;s the most important lesson you&rsquo;ve learned in your career so far?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"mc md ch ap me b mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo mp\" id=\"43ae\">I&rsquo;ve been leading software product teams all over the world for over 20 years now. I&rsquo;ve had the benefit of having worked for very large companies (Microsoft), small companies (Cactus, Ascentium), startups (CommerceServer.net), and medium sized/high growth companies (Hootsuite and Sitecore). And I&rsquo;ve done it across many geographies and cultures including the United States, Canada, United Kingdom, Denmark, Belgium, Netherlands, Ukraine, Malaysia, India, Australia, and China (and I unfortunately have the frequent flier miles to prove it.)</p>\n\n<p class=\"mc md ch ap me b mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo mp\" id=\"9766\">Across these varied journeys, one key lesson emerges &mdash; context matters! When making decisions or making changes, you have to consider the complete picture that includes both the business circumstances, organizational history, culture, and the people involved. Failing to keep all three in balance can often result in a lot of proverbial &ldquo;gear grinding&rdquo; and frustration in addition to hindered progress.</p>\n\n<p class=\"mc md ch ap me b mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo mp\" id=\"f617\"><strong class=\"me mq\">Where do you see the greatest area of opportunity for Hootsuite?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"mc md ch ap me b mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo mp\" id=\"8251\">Social is at the forefront of digital marketing today, above virtually all other categories of marketing technology priorities for CMOs. It is positioned to grow even bigger as it takes over more traditional means of brand: customer interactions, such as call centers or e-mail queues.</p>\n\n<p class=\"mc md ch ap me b mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo mp\" id=\"65e3\">Hootsuite is already the leader in social media management and the company is positioned to be at the absolute forefront of what is going to be one of the hottest topics in marketing technology for the next decade and beyond.</p>\n\n<p class=\"mc md ch ap me b mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo mp\" id=\"7211\"><strong class=\"me mq\">What excites you most about what is next for Product at Hootsuite?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"mc md ch ap me b mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo mp\" id=\"0845\">The product is the heart and soul of Hootsuite; it is what our customers use all day, every day. Given the aforementioned market opportunity, at Hootsuite we have the opportunity to not only impact the lives of millions of digital marketers &mdash; but to affect millions of brand-customer interactions.</p>\n\n<p class=\"mc md ch ap me b mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo mp\" id=\"009e\">Working in product at Hootsuite is an absolutely amazing opportunity to be at the intersection of amazing digital marketing innovation as well as have the opportunity to work with the latest and greatest cloud technologies.</p>\n\n<figure class=\"lj lk ll lm ln ev lo lp paragraph-image\">\n<div class=\"x y nu\">\n<div class=\"lw l ej lx\">\n<div class=\"nv l\">\n<div class=\"do lt gi n o gh ab bx lu lv\"><img alt=\"undefined\" src=\"https://cdn.phenompeople.com/CareerConnectResources/HOOTUS/images/RD-blog-sitting-1579605563304.jpeg\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto;\" /></div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</figure>\n\n<p class=\"mc md ch ap me b mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo mp\" id=\"c8e2\"><strong class=\"me mq\">What&rsquo;s the most important trait someone on your team needs to have?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"mc md ch ap me b mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo mp\" id=\"831a\">I&rsquo;m going to cheat and answer with a balance of three key traits: passion, curiosity, and respect. Based on my experience, the healthiest, happiest, and highest performing teams are comprised of individuals that are strong and well-balanced in all three key traits. Having a diverse and balanced team helps to eliminate other challenges that one sees from time-to-time, such as &ldquo;brilliant jerks&rdquo; or a lack of passion to innovate.</p>\n\n<p class=\"mc md ch ap me b mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo mp\" id=\"d0f3\"><strong class=\"me mq\">How do you see the industry changing in the next 5 years?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"mc md ch ap me b mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo mp\" id=\"b9a2\">The marketing technology industry is going to continue its crazy pace of hyper-evolution. Digital experience platforms will mature and commoditize to accommodate the Web and Mobile presences of brands. More traditional means of customer contact, such as call centres, CRM, and e-mail will shrink in usage.</p>\n\n<p class=\"mc md ch ap me b mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo mp\" id=\"bff4\">Taking its place will be social, which will result in the principal means of customers interacting with brands. I know in my own life I see more of the brands I care about on social than I do through more traditional means these days. I have been a very frequent flier of United Airlines, and I see far more of them on Instagram or Facebook than I do except when I&rsquo;m buying a ticket or actually on a plane. And who would want to pick up a phone when you could iMessage or WhatsApp instead? With my busy schedule, picking up the phone is an inconvenience as it literally requires blocking a slot off on the calendar that I&rsquo;d rather put towards customers or the team. And in the event of a customer service crisis, a brand is held accountable via social &mdash; which has never happened with more traditional means of contact. And in that case, the consumer significantly benefits.</p>\n\n<p class=\"mc md ch ap me b mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo mp\" id=\"1847\">What this is going to do is create an innovation &ldquo;arms race&rdquo; between the social networks themselves and for social technology players to help brands most effectively manage their presences. As with most categories, social technology will likely end up in an oligopoly with a handful of dominant players as has occurred in most other categories such as CRM, content and commerce platforms. With its size, history, and position of market leadership, Hootsuite is very well positioned to be at the absolute forefront of the social technology space.</p>\n\n<blockquote class=\"ne\">\n<div class=\"nf ng nh ap jn b ke ni nj nk nl nm mp\" id=\"81d7\">\n<p class=\"jn b nn no at\">&ldquo;Everyone should have a clear development plan with training, stretch assignments, etc. that help them realize their potential and career aspirations.&rdquo;</p>\n</div>\n</blockquote>\n\n<figure class=\"nx ny nz oa ob ev gf oc br od oe of og oh bc oi oj ok ol om on paragraph-image\">\n<div class=\"lq lr ej ls ab\">\n<div class=\"x y nw\">\n<div class=\"lw l ej lx\">\n<div class=\"oo l\">\n<div class=\"do lt gi n o gh ab bx lu lv\"><img alt=\"\" class=\"gi n o gh ab lz ma mb\" height=\"4000\" role=\"presentation\" src=\"https://miro.medium.com/1*om9DW8Ty8g3xMYTLRSi7cQ.jpeg?q=20\" style=\"max-height: 400px;max-width: 100%;\" width=\"4000\" /></div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</figure>\n\n<p class=\"mc md ch ap me b mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo mp\" id=\"1cbe\"><strong class=\"me mq\">How do you build and develop your team of talent to ensure everyone is at their best?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"mc md ch ap me b mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo mp\" id=\"7a15\">To ensure that everyone is at their best and have an inclusive, diverse workplace where people can have fun over the long-term, a couple of key elements need to be in place. First and foremost, there has to be clear roles, responsibilities, and expectations. Second, there has to be a very clear mission. From there, I believe in having very clear expectations for progression both within a given role as well as clear steps for someone to transition to another role as part of their career development.</p>\n\n<p class=\"mc md ch ap me b mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo mp\" id=\"bfdd\">Everyone should have a clear development plan with training, stretch assignments, etc. that help them realize their potential and career aspirations. This requires a significant investment in people, but it absolutely pays huge dividends over time. This is especially true in high growth environments where the needs are ever-expanding.</p>\n\n<p class=\"mc md ch ap me b mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo mp\" id=\"49f4\"><strong class=\"me mq\">What does company culture mean to you?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"mc md ch ap me b mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo mp\" id=\"44e3\">I view company culture as a blend of the company&rsquo;s mission and purpose, values, people, and success metrics. Those elements together combine to create the culture of daily life within the organization. In my 20+ year career in the technology industry, Hootsuite has one of the clearest (and aspirational) missions and corporate values combined with an amazingly talented workforce and ever-maturing success metrics.</p>\n\n<p class=\"mc md ch ap me b mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo mp\" id=\"b9c9\">So far, I&rsquo;ve found the culture to be amazing and I am having a blast each and every day. When I joined Hootsuite, I was worried that I had over-hyped my own mental expectations; instead, I have had them pleasantly exceeded each and every day.</p>\n\n<p class=\"mc md ch ap me b mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo mp\" id=\"c8d9\"><strong class=\"me mq\">How would you define your leadership style?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"mc md ch ap me b mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo mp\" id=\"c3b2\">I believe in creating teams where people can achieve their personal and professional goals while achieving amazing business results &mdash; and having a lot of fun at the same time. To make this happen, I believe in the concept of empowered accountability coupled with clear support from me as a leader. It is my job as an executive to ensure that expectations, roles, and responsibilities are crystal clear. This just eliminates ambiguity and chaos.</p>\n\n<p class=\"mc md ch ap me b mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo mp\" id=\"c4d4\">Next, I am here to help in any capacity that is required. That can be serving as a sounding board, unblocking something cross-organizationally, or helping to facilitate collaboration.</p>\n\n<p class=\"mc md ch ap me b mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo mp\" id=\"20da\">Third, I am here to help develop the careers of each and everyone in my team. This is often a mix of mentorship, creating stretch assignments, ensuring access to training, or whatever else is required to help my team achieve their career aspirations.</p>\n\n<p class=\"mc md ch ap me b mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo mp\" id=\"05aa\"><strong class=\"me mq\">What do you do when you&rsquo;re not in the office?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"mc md ch ap me b mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo mp\" id=\"3b5b\">First, I have a lovely wife who is a senior software engineering executive for another high growth technology company. She manages a global team spanning four countries with her anchor point being in the United Kingdom. So yes, we have been living in separate countries for several years which makes things a bit complicated but does make for some interesting travel meetups. I am extremely proud and supportive of her!</p>\n\n<figure class=\"ms ev op mu lp lo mv paragraph-image\">\n<div class=\"lq lr ej ls ab\">\n<div class=\"lw l ej lx\">\n<div class=\"oq l\">\n<div class=\"do lt gi n o gh ab bx lu lv\"><img alt=\"undefined\" src=\"https://cdn.phenompeople.com/CareerConnectResources/HOOTUS/images/RD-blog-dogs-1579607833446.jpeg\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto;\" /></div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</figure>\n\n<figure class=\"ms ev or mu lp lo mv paragraph-image\">\n<div class=\"lq lr ej ls ab\">\n<div class=\"lw l ej lx\">\n<div class=\"mw l\">\n<div class=\"do lt gi n o gh ab bx lu lv\"><img alt=\"undefined\" src=\"https://cdn.phenompeople.com/CareerConnectResources/HOOTUS/images/RD-blog-cars-1579607873741.jpeg\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto;\" /></div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</figure>\n\n<p class=\"mc md ch ap me b mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo mp\" id=\"96c3\">We have two dachshunds, whom I adore and truly enjoy spoiling. For hobbies, I am an enthusiast of architecture and landscape photography and classic British cars. I am also a voracious reader. I tend to mix up keeping up with my social feeds, world news, technology and industry news, business best practices, and novels (a mix of mysteries, historical fiction, and drama/suspense).</p>\n\n<hr class=\"os cy gz ot ou hj ov ow ox oy oz\" />\n<h2 class=\"pa pb ch ap ao bz pc pd pe pf pg ph pi pj pk pl pm\" id=\"4d05\"><strong class=\"bb\">Did I mention we&rsquo;re hiring?
