6},"width":{"type":"text","value":1440},"focalPointY":{"type":"text","value":0},"lqip":{"type":"text","value":null},"height":{"type":"text","value":956},"focalPointX":{"type":"text","value":0}}},"alt":{"type":"text","value":"sheryl-blog"}}},"ogTitle":{"type":"text","value":null},"description":{"type":"text","value":"Meet Sheryl, Senior Director of Product Design at Hootsuite"},"title":{"type":"text","value":"Meet Sheryl, Senior Director of Product Design at Hootsuite"},"body":{"type":"text","value":"<h1 class=\"jn b jo jv ch\"><span style=\"color:rgba(0, 0, 0, 1);\"><strong class=\"bb\">Meet Sheryl, Senior Director of Product Design at Hootsuite</strong></span></h1>\n\n<h2 class=\"ao cy ke kf at\">What does it look like to work in product design at Hootsuite? In this interview, we learn about Sheryl&rsquo;s perspective including motherhood, risk-taking, and leadership lessons.</h2>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"a450\"><strong class=\"lu mg\">What are you responsible for at Hootsuite?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"628a\">As the Senior Director of Product Design, I lead and mentor an amazingly talented team of over 20 <a class=\"dc bt mh mi mj mk\" href=\"https://careers.hootsuite.com/global/en/product-management-design\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\">User Experience Designers and User Researchers</a>, across our Vancouver, Toronto, Bucharest and Milan offices. Together, we&rsquo;re responsible for championing the voice of our customer, and ultimately delivering a super intuitive and thoughtful user experience for our customers.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"a9ac\">I also work closely with the VP of Product, and the VP of Development to drive alignment, and foster happy, healthy, collaborative relationships across our teams, portfolios and across other departments. We develop longer term vision and strategy for the Hootsuite Product, and help our teams successfully execute on the Product Roadmap.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"e432\"><strong class=\"lu mg\">Why did you join Hootsuite?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"2f2a\">In 2015, I made a somewhat crazy decision to give up my career at Google in the Bay Area, and move to Vancouver in search for that elusive work/life balance. When looking at opportunities, I was really eager to find a working environment that had a similar feel to Google &mdash; in terms of its values, its culture, its spirit &mdash; and I wanted to surround myself with passionate and talented people that I could learn from. I also wanted to operate in a domain that was dynamic and innovative. Hootsuite was that for me.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"8553\">When I first joined back in 2015 as a Senior UX Designer, the Product Design team was a small group of around 8, and they operated in a client-services model. I knew I was stepping into an engineering-led environment where design was viewed as an afterthought &mdash; which is very typical for a startup &mdash; but I was excited by the challenge of changing that model to be more customer-centric and design-led. And when I joined, I found so many amazing allies within the organization who were already chipping away at shifting the way we worked, and slowly but surely, we&rsquo;ve brought the customer into the center of all we do! :)</p>\n\n<blockquote class=\"ml\">\n<div class=\"mm mn mo ap jn b ke mp mq mr ms mt mf\" id=\"80d1\">\n<p class=\"jn b mu mv at\">&ldquo;What&rsquo;s unique about the way we operate is that UX Designers at Hootsuite are seen as true partners in developing and executing on the strategy and roadmap for Hootsuite Product.&rdquo;</p>\n</div>\n</blockquote>\n\n<figure class=\"mw mx my mz na ev x y paragraph-image\">\n<div class=\"lg lh ej li ab\">\n<div class=\"x y la\">\n<div class=\"lm l ej ln\">\n<div class=\"nb l\" style=\"width:100%;height:100%;min-height:100% !important;\">\n<div class=\"do lj gi n o gh ab bx lk ll\">&nbsp;</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n\n<figcaption class=\"at eb nc nd hj dm x y ne nf ao cy\"><img alt=\"undefined\" src=\"https://cdn.phenompeople.com/CareerConnectResources/HOOTUS/images/sheryl-blog-team-1579603875177.jpeg\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto;\" />Some of my amazing team!</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"9102\"><strong class=\"lu mg\">How would you describe your team?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"6be2\">My team is best described as my extended family &mdash; they are supportive, inspiring, passionate, kind, awesome human beings &mdash; and just absolutely amazing at what they do. We are a very close-knit bunch who are super passionate about building customer empathy in the organization through user research, data and insights, and delivering thoughtful and well-crafted user experiences. And we have a lot of fun doing it!</p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"8112\">What&rsquo;s unique about the way we operate is that UX Designers at Hootsuite are seen as true partners in developing and executing on the strategy and roadmap for Hootsuite Product. We don&rsquo;t just respond to a design brief that&rsquo;s been thrown over a fence by a Product Manager. We are actively involved in helping understand the problem space, we help teams build customer empathy, and together with the triad, we collaborate closely on driving Product strategy.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"e8ab\">I am extremely proud of how the team has grown over the years &mdash; not only in size (we&rsquo;ve more than doubled!) &mdash; but in the level of influence they have within the organization. The team has been instrumental in shifting our culture to be one that is more customer-centric and design-led. We&rsquo;ve shifted from a client-services model into an integrated model &mdash; where we have UX designers embedded within each Product portfolio team. And I have had the immense pleasure of witnessing the growth and development of my team and colleagues as designers and as leaders.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"0f85\"><strong class=\"lu mg\">What is one project you&rsquo;re particularly proud of your team for?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"a75d\">One of the most notable recent accomplishments from my team is the collaborative development of our Customer Personas and User Journey map. In 2018, the User Research team worked very closely with their counterparts in Marketing and Sales to build a robust and consolidated view of our Customers, and operationalized these Customer Personas across the organization. In a company as large as Hootsuite, that is a major accomplishment, and really set a strong foundation for building Customer empathy. This year, the Product Design team have extended that work by diving deep into outlining our user&rsquo;s journey, their tasks and workflows &mdash; documenting and sharing this knowledge across the Product organization. As part of this, we&rsquo;ve developed collaborative &ldquo;Portfolio Guidebooks&rdquo; &mdash; which centralizes all of our shared knowledge about our customers, the problem space, the market landscape, and our vision and strategy for a portfolio. This is just one example of how my team drives alignment and cohesion across the Product Suite.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"8c08\"><strong class=\"lu mg\">Why is now an exciting time to be on your team?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"c096\">With our new SVP of Product, <a class=\"dc bt mh mi mj mk\" href=\"/hootsuite-careers/visionary-and-tech-industry-veteran-meet-hootsuites-senior-vice-president-of-product-and-909b9a94d8f9\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\">Ryan Donovan</a> at the helm, it&rsquo;s been super exciting to have the importance of user-experience design elevated and championed at the executive level. The Product Design team have a bold and exciting challenge ahead to truly make our product&rsquo;s user experience a differentiator within the realm of social media management.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\"><img alt=\"undefined\" src=\"https://cdn.phenompeople.com/CareerConnectResources/HOOTUS/images/sheryl-blog-google-1579603926329.jpeg\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto;\" /></p>\n\n<figure class=\"lb lc ld le lf ev x y paragraph-image\">\n<div class=\"lg lh ej li ab\">\n<div class=\"x y la\">\n<div class=\"lm l ej ln\">\n<div class=\"ng l\">\n<div class=\"do lj gi n o gh ab bx lk ll\">&nbsp;</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</figure>\n\n<blockquote class=\"ml\">\n<div class=\"mm mn mo ap jn b ke mp mq mr ms mt mf\" id=\"9b55\">\n<p class=\"jn b mu mv at\">&ldquo;a huge part of being a strong leader is having the humility to recognize your own shortcomings and areas for growth, being open and honest about them, and not being afraid to ask for help.&rdquo;</p>\n</div>\n</blockquote>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv nh lx ni lz nj mb nk md nl mf\" id=\"32db\"><strong class=\"lu mg\">What are the unique challenges about working on your team?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"c725\">One of the unique challenges about our team is based on the way our teams are structured. Because we have UX designers integrated into each Product portfolio, they develop a strong vertical expertise within their domain.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"b3fb\">However, in order to deliver a cohesive and holistic user experience across the entire Product suite, our UX designers also need to ensure they are also aware of what each other are working on, and collaborate closely when necessary. It&rsquo;s a unique balance to ensure each team can function independently, but also maintains alignment and delivers a cohesive and unified Product experience.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"b2eb\"><strong class=\"lu mg\">Share with us a valuable leadership lesson.</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"c057\">I started my career at Hootsuite as one of the UX Designers on the Product Design team, and so when I was promoted into the role of Director, I had to transition from being an individual contributor, to being a manager and leader.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"ce30\">Early into the transition, I was lucky enough to be involved in a leadership training session that introduced the concept of self-protective strategies. I recognized that one of my own self-protective strategies I tended to revert to was &ldquo;martyrdom&rdquo;. Martyrdom is where you struggle to give up control, with a &ldquo;I&rsquo;ll do it then&rdquo; mentality and an internal story of &ldquo;I&rsquo;m the only one who can do this properly&rdquo;. Becoming aware of my own self-protective strategies forced me to take a long, hard look at how I was showing up as a leader, and some of the unintended consequences that could arise as a result.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"6ffe\">I immediately shared my own self-protective strategies with my team. And as a result, I recognized that I couldn&rsquo;t (and shouldn&rsquo;t) do everything on my own. I learned to trust my team to help me get the job done. And by supporting and empowering them, I witnessed them grow and succeed as designers and leaders &mdash; and this by far is one of the most fulfilling and rewarding aspects of my job.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"ec48\">This was a valuable leadership lesson I learned early on: a huge part of being a strong leader is having the humility to recognize your own shortcomings and areas for growth, being open and honest about them, and not being afraid to ask for help.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"c8a5\"><strong class=\"lu mg\">What or who inspires you?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"b2be\">I recently became a mother &mdash; and it may sound cliche, but I can honestly say that my baby boy Finn (who is now 18 months &mdash; where did the time go?!) has completely changed my perspective of the world. Having a kid makes you view the world differently. You reassess what&rsquo;s really important in life. Time suddenly takes on a different meaning &mdash; a year feels ridiculously short. Finn has made me realize the importance of living for the now, being present in the moment, and not dwelling on the past, or stressing about the future. He&rsquo;s made me think about the kind of world I want him to live in, and about the kind of example I want to set for him.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"f2b4\">So when I returned back to work at the beginning of the year, it wasn&rsquo;t without trepidation &mdash; and it&rsquo;s definitely been challenging balancing my career with motherhood. But I am thankful for the flexible work environment at Hootsuite, and for my team who have been super supportive. It&rsquo;s made me more hyper-conscious of what it means to be a woman in tech, and a mother in tech, and some of the unique challenges we face. I would say I am probably more inspired than ever to be a strong and successful example of a woman in leadership, in the tech industry.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"9ae0\"><strong class=\"lu mg\">What&rsquo;s the biggest risk you&rsquo;ve ever taken in your career and how did it pay off?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"16fd\">In 2012, I was faced with a major fork in the road for my career and life. I was offered a UX Director role at a major Advertising agency in Sydney, but I decided to turn it down and relocate to San Francisco instead, as a Senior UX Designer at frog design.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"35ae\">Though the role as a UX Director would have been a bigger &ldquo;career jump&rdquo;, I turned it down because I felt like I still had a lot of growth I wanted to do as a UX designer, and I didn&rsquo;t feel quite ready to be in a leadership position at the time. Not that moving halfway across the world, to a city I&rsquo;ve never even visited before was any easier! ;) As much as I was eager for rapid career growth, it was a very important decision that I made to slow down, and really assess what I needed for my own development and career success.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"4f36\">And it did pay off. What I gained through my experience living abroad in SF for 3 years was incomparable. I got to meet, learn from and be mentored by some of the brightest and most talented people in the Bay Area, whilst working with some huge international brands on very cool and emerging tech. And it led to me landing that coveted dream job at Google, where I got to work in the crazy field of Robotics.</p>\n\n<p class=\"ls lt ch ap lu b lv lw lx ly lz ma mb mc md me mf\" id=\"e86d\">In time, my career growth did eventually veer towards a leadership position again- but rather than prematurely stepping into a role I knew I wasn&rsquo;t prepared for, I got to step into leadership at a time where I felt confident and prepared for the challenges ahead.</p>\n\n<hr class=\"nm cy gz nn no hj np nq nr ns nt\" />\n<h2 class=\"nu nv ch ap ao bz nw nx ny nz oa ob oc od oe of og\" id=\"1d29\">Interested in taking on new challenges at Hootsuite? <a class=\"dc bt mh mi mj mk\" href=\"https://careers.hootsuite.com/global/en/product-management-design\" rel=\"noopener\" Ken, Senior Director of Software Development at Hootsuite"},"title":{"type":"text","value":"Meet Ken, Senior Director of Software Development at Hootsuite"},"body":{"type":"text","value":"<h1 class=\"jn b jo jv ch\">Meet Ken, Senior Director of Software Development at Hootsuite</h1>\n\n<h2 class=\"ao cy ke kf at\">Interested in working in Software Development at Hootsuite? Learn more about the team and why now is the time to join.</h2>\n\n<p>&nbsp;</p>\n\n<figure class=\"lb lc ld le lf ev gf lg br lh li lj lk ll bc lm ln lo lp lq lr paragraph-image\">\n<div class=\"x y la\">\n<div class=\"lv l ej lw\">\n<div class=\"lx l\">\n<div class=\"do ls gi n o gh ab bx lt lu\"><img alt=\"undefined\" src=\"https://cdn.phenompeople.com/CareerConnectResources/HOOTUS/images/ken-blog-1579603037962.jpeg\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto;\" /></div>\n\n<div class=\"do ls gi n o gh ab bx lt lu\">&nbsp;</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</figure>\n\n<p class=\"mb mc ch ap md b me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo\" id=\"00f3\"><strong class=\"md mp\">What are you responsible for at Hootsuite?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"mb mc ch ap md b me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo\" id=\"163b\">My role at Hootsuite is Senior Director of Software Development.</p>\n\n<p class=\"mb mc ch ap md b me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo\" id=\"8b4f\">I manage the dev teams that build and maintain our social marketing and social customer support tools &mdash; these are the tools our customers use to build their brand and connect with their customers.</p>\n\n<p class=\"mb mc ch ap md b me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo\" id=\"2689\"><strong class=\"md mp\">Why did you choose to join Hootsuite?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"mb mc ch ap md b me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo\" id=\"3033\">I joined Hootsuite 6 years ago when we were still very much in startup mode. The fun culture and opportunity to work with a growing, healthy, private Canadian tech company was very attractive to me.</p>\n\n<p class=\"mb mc ch ap md b me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo\" id=\"a804\">I&rsquo;ve seen Hootsuite grow up and I feel blessed to have experienced some of the early craziness as well as the maturation and global success. The Hootsuite of 2019 is a more diverse and inclusive organization and we&rsquo;re getting much better at both understanding and meeting the needs of our customers.</p>\n\n<p class=\"mb mc ch ap md b me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo\" id=\"a5b5\"><strong class=\"md mp\">Describe your team.</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"mb mc ch ap md b me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo\" id=\"5742\">I have two teams of about 25 developers. We work closely with Product &amp; Design partners to plan, design &amp; deliver valuable features and reliability to our customers.</p>\n\n<p class=\"mb mc ch ap md b me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo\" id=\"aa68\">Over the past few years, we&rsquo;ve replaced a number of legacy components with new &amp; better versions. Two examples of this are New Compose and Planner &mdash; replacements for core social marketing components that are more feature-rich, more reliable and more extensible than their predecessors. We&rsquo;ve tackled a number of interesting UX and technical challenges to do this and we&rsquo;re now at a point where we can build on these platforms to create amazing experiences for our customers.</p>\n\n<p class=\"mb mc ch ap md b me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo\">&nbsp;</p>\n\n<figure class=\"lb lc ld le lf ev x y paragraph-image\">\n<div class=\"x y mq\">\n<div class=\"lv l ej lw\">\n<div class=\"mr l\">\n<div class=\"do ls gi n o gh ab bx lt lu\"><img alt=\"undefined\" src=\"https://cdn.phenompeople.com/CareerConnectResources/HOOTUS/images/ken-blog-team-1579603086037.jpeg\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto;\" /></div>\n\n<div class=\"do ls gi n o gh ab bx lt lu\">&nbsp;</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n\n<figcaption class=\"at eb ms mt hj dm x y mu mv ao cy\">On a team outing making ceramics!</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\n<p class=\"mb mc ch ap md b me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo\" id=\"5827\"><strong class=\"md mp\">Hootsuite deemed 2019 as the &ldquo;</strong><a class=\"dc bt mw mx my mz\" href=\"/hootsuite-careers/leading-the-charge-through-the-year-of-the-product-2301179a58dc\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\"><strong class=\"md mp\">Year of Product.</strong></a><strong class=\"md mp\">&rdquo; How will you and your team contribute to this?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"mb mc ch ap md b me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo\" id=\"e777\">In 2019 I&rsquo;m leading our Reliability &amp; Performance corporate initiative, where we&rsquo;re making significant investments in the reliability &amp; performance of our products. We have a passion for customer success and it&rsquo;s clear that our customers need a highly performant and reliable product to achieve their goals. This year we&rsquo;re making that happen.</p>\n\n<p class=\"mb mc ch ap md b me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo\" id=\"c977\">All our dev teams are contributing to this by defining and achieving Service Level Objectives (SLOs) and Error Budget Policies for their portfolios. These agreements give us a clear understanding of our customer&rsquo;s needs, a real-time, data-driven view of their experience, and clear expectations about when it&rsquo;s time to invest in reliability.</p>\n\n<p class=\"mb mc ch ap md b me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo\" id=\"d7a0\"><strong class=\"md mp\">What are some of the technologies your team works with?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"mb mc ch ap md b me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo\" id=\"e46c\">We have a fantastic continuous integration &amp; delivery (CI/CD) system that allows our dev teams to ship code to our production Kubernetes cluster many times a day. Once features are out, we use industry best-practices from SRE like SLOs and Error Budgets to ensure that our systems remain reliable and performant.</p>\n\n<p class=\"mb mc ch ap md b me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo\" id=\"734c\">We&rsquo;re committed to Observability and we work closely with our SRE team to ensure that our Mongo and MySQL databases are properly configured, our Scala and Go services are scaled out to meet growing customer needs, and our legacy PHP system remains stable amidst all the change.</p>\n\n<figure class=\"lr ls lt lu lv fw x y paragraph-image\">\n<div class=\"no np bi nq ab\">\n<div class=\"x y ne\">\n<div class=\"mj l bi mk\"><img alt=\"undefined\" src=\"https://cdn.phenompeople.com/CareerConnectResources/HOOTUS/images/ken-blog-outside-1579603118737.jpeg\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto;\" /></div>\n\n<div class=\"mj l bi mk\">&nbsp;</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</figure>\n\n<p class=\"mb mc ch ap md b me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo\" id=\"4f6a\"><strong class=\"md mp\">Why is NOW an exciting time to be on your team?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"mb mc ch ap md b me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo\" id=\"d231\">Over the past 10 years we&rsquo;ve built an amazing product with a broad set of features. Our customers love it and the business grows every day.</p>\n\n<p class=\"mb mc ch ap md b me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo\" id=\"0526\">With the current focus on strong social core and reliability, we are taking the opportunity to reinvest in core functionality and make it even better. We will be doing everything from fixing broken UI / UX to improving the reliability and performance of web, service and infrastructure components. Everyone has a great opportunity to take on interesting projects, solve unique problems and make a substantial impact.</p>\n\n<p class=\"mb mc ch ap md b me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo\" id=\"9df1\"><strong class=\"md mp\">What are the unique challenges about working on your team?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"mb mc ch ap md b me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo\" id=\"0657\">The two main challenges that face my team at the moment, and it takes every one of us to work collaboratively to accomplish the pretty big goals we&rsquo;ve set for ourselves. They are:</p>\n\n<p class=\"mb mc ch ap md b me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo\" id=\"fb72\">Scale: My team is responsible for publishing all our customer&rsquo;s messages &mdash; both ad-hoc and scheduled &mdash; in a timely manner to all our supported channels. In order to do this well our services and infrastructure to be reliable, scalable and highly observable.</p>\n\n<p class=\"mb mc ch ap md b me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo\" id=\"a445\">Impact: Working on core product means there&rsquo;s always more to do than time to do it. We need to ensure that all our projects &mdash; technical and features &mdash; are highly impactful for our customers.</p>\n\n<p class=\"mb mc ch ap md b me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo\">&nbsp;</p>\n\n<figure class=\"nn ev no np nq nr ns paragraph-image\">\n<div class=\"lv l ej lw\">\n<div class=\"nt l\">\n<div class=\"do ls gi n o gh ab bx lt lu\"><img alt=\"undefined\" src=\"https://cdn.phenompeople.com/CareerConnectResources/HOOTUS/images/ken-blog-winter-1579603256913.jpeg\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto;\" /></div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</figure>\n\n<figure class=\"nn ev nu np nq nr ns paragraph-image\">\n<div class=\"na nb ej nc ab\">\n<div class=\"lv l ej lw\">\n<div class=\"nv l\">\n<div class=\"do ls gi n o gh ab bx lt lu\"><img alt=\"undefined\" src=\"https://cdn.phenompeople.com/CareerConnectResources/HOOTUS/images/ken-blog-lake-1579603296943.jpeg\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto;\" /></div>\n\n<div class=\"do ls gi n o gh ab bx lt lu\">&nbsp;</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n\n<figcaption class=\"at eb ms mt hj dm x y mu mv ao cy nw ej nx ny\">Enjoying the outdoors no matter the conditions :)</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\n<p class=\"mb mc ch ap md b me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo\" id=\"99a6\"><strong class=\"md mp\">What are three things you would tell someone starting a job at Hootsuite?</strong></p>\n\n<ol>\n\t<li class=\"mb mc ch ap md b me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo nz oa ob\" id=\"0241\">The people are amazing.</li>\n\t<li class=\"mb mc ch ap md b me oc mg od mi oe mk of mm og mo nz oa ob\" id=\"d606\">The market opportunity is huge.</li>\n\t<li class=\"mb mc ch ap md b me oc mg od mi oe mk of mm og mo nz oa ob\" id=\"54ef\">Working for Hootsuite is different than working at one of the big companies in Vancouver. We are in a sweet spot right now where we are big enough to work on super interesting projects, and small enough that you get to have a very direct influence on the success of our products and business.</li>\n</ol>\n\n<p class=\"mb mc ch ap md b me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo\" id=\"f503\"><strong class=\"md mp\">What or who inspires you?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"mb mc ch ap md b me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo\" id=\"2f75\">I love spending time in nature and Vancouver is a great place for me to do it!</p>\n\n<p class=\"mb mc ch ap md b me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo\" id=\"f682\"><strong class=\"md mp\">What&rsquo;s your secret talent that no one knows about?</strong></p>\n\n<p class=\"mb mc ch ap md b me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo\" id=\"64de\">I&rsquo;m an avid meditator and try to spend 10 days a year on silent retreats. Retreats are a lot of work but are amazing for personal growth and development.</p>\n\n<hr class=\"oh cy gz oi oj hj ok ol om on oo\" />\n<p class=\"mb mc ch ap md b me mf mg mh mi mj mk ml mm mn mo\" id=\"06e6\"><strong class=\"md mp\">Join my team! Hootsuite"},"title":{"type":"text","value":"Joining Hootsuite"},"body":{"type":"text","value":"<h1 class=\"jn b jo jv ch\">Joining Hootsuite</h1>\n\n<p class=\"lj lk ch ap ll b lm ln lo lp lq lr ls lt lu lv lw\" id=\"3e8e\">I&rsquo;m very excited to share that I&rsquo;ve recently joined Hootsuite as Senior Director of Product. Hootsuite pioneered the social media dashboard and is now the most widely used social media management platform in the world, trusted by more than 16 million people and employees at 80% of the Fortune 1000.</p>\n\n<p class=\"lj lk ch ap ll b lm ln lo lp lq lr ls lt lu lv lw\" id=\"7348\">Over my entire adult life, I&rsquo;ve had the privilege of working with smart and creative people on solving problems at the intersection of technology and customer experience. I first became fascinated with the Internet while helping my parents with their small business marketing and IT when I was 12 years old and I have been immersed in the world of social media &mdash; particularly how brands and people interact online &mdash; ever since I first experienced The Facebook while in college. Over that time, social media have completely transformed how we learn about, consider, choose, buy, and tell our friends about brands and products.</p>\n\n<p class=\"lj lk ch ap ll b lm ln lo lp lq lr ls lt lu lv lw\" id=\"fb23\">At Vancouver-based Hootsuite, I&rsquo;ll be working with over 1000 people who are just as passionate about social media&rsquo;s role in business and our society as I am. Hootsuite has evolved over the years while always staying true to its roots. The company&rsquo;s purpose is to champion the power of human connection, and we take this to heart.</p>\n\n<p class=\"lj lk ch ap ll b lm ln lo lp lq lr ls lt lu lv lw\" id=\"557b\">We want to empower all organizations &mdash; large and small &mdash; to strategically grow their brand, business and customer relationships with social. From Forrester naming Hootsuite a leader for cementing its &lsquo;enterprise status&rsquo; in the 2017 Social Wave &mdash; to thousands of positive reviews on sites like G2 Crowd &mdash; Hootsuite has made great strides by focusing on its mission and aligning around customer needs in a rapidly changing social landscape.</p>\n\n<p class=\"lj lk ch ap ll b lm ln lo lp lq lr ls lt lu lv lw\" id=\"6f93\">As one of the pioneers in software as a service for marketers, advertisers, salespeople, and customer care teams &mdash; Hootsuite has just celebrated its 10th anniversary. Alas, we are looking ahead at what the future of social marketing, advertising, sales, and customer service looks like. We are not concerned with innovating for the sake of innovating or growing for the sake of growing. At Hootsuite, we are focused on understanding the reality in which our customers operate &mdash; and making sure our platform helps them serve their customers.</p>\n\n<p class=\"lj lk ch ap ll b lm ln lo lp lq lr ls lt lu lv lw\" id=\"a3d4\">In my new role, I&rsquo;ll be helping the Hootsuite product team to continue to move with customer-centricity. There is much we are proud of, and yet so much left for us to do. And so much we can improve and learn from. The past decade was just the beginning; we strive to continuously build on a social media management platform that is not only powerful and comprehensive but also enjoyable, efficient, and easy to use. You can expect much from us in the year to come.</p>\n\n<p class=\"lj lk ch ap ll b lm ln lo lp lq lr ls lt lu lv lw\" id=\"5339\">You can count on Hootsuite continuing to move forward by putting customers first. You can count on us living by our core values: &lsquo;<em class=\"lx\">Passion for customer success</em>,&rsquo; &lsquo;<em class=\"lx\">Lead with humility</em>,&rsquo; &lsquo;<em class=\"lx\">Build a better way</em>,&rsquo; and &lsquo;<em class=\"lx\">Grit in all we do</em>.&rsquo; You can count on us ensuring the lovability of our brand &mdash; as always manifested by our mascot Owly &mdash; to translate to each pixel, each line of code, and each interaction with our team members. You can count on us to think about privacy, ethics, and compliance by design; never as an afterthought. You can count on an expanding ecosystem of third-party apps and partners. You can count on us to be at the forefront of identifying trends and facilitating the social customer journey. And you can count on the Hootsuite platform to help you build your brand, strengthen your relationship with customers, integrate social across your organization, and drive meaningful business results with social.</p>\n\n<p class=\"lj lk ch ap ll b lm ln lo lp lq lr ls lt lu lv lw\" id=\"9c72\">I&rsquo;m grateful for this new opportunity and cannot wait to share more about what we&rsquo;re building at the owl nest. If you&rsquo;re already using Hootsuite or are thinking about it for your team &mdash; please feel free to reach out with your suggestions and feedback. You can find me on Twitter <a class=\"dc bt ly lz ma mb\" href=\"http://www.twitter.com/socialnerdia\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\">@socialnerdia</a>.</p>\n\n<p class=\"lj lk ch ap ll b lm ln lo lp lq lr ls lt lu lv lw\" id=\"8539\">Ps. <a class=\"dc bt ly lz ma mb\" href=\"http://ow.ly/rqvX30mRK3G\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\">We&rsquo;re hiring.</a></p>\n\n<p class=\"lj lk ch ap ll b lm ln lo lp lq lr ls lt lu lv lw\" id=\"3127\">-Esteban
